)@@G@@    BK1 AND BK2.  THIS PROCESSOR, WHEN CALLED AFTER THE PRINT FILE HAS  EZ
)@@G@@@H@@@@.         BEEN DIVERTED VIA BK1, WILL RETURN THE PRINT FILE TO THEFA

)@@G@@    IS SPECIFIED AND THE FILE IS TEMPORARY, AN ERROR MESSAGE WILL @H@@@@FH
)@@G@@.         BE GIVEN.  IF THE SITE IS OMITTED, THE PRINT WILL BE DIRECTED FI
)@@G@@TO    @G@@@@.         THE IMPLIED OUTPUT DEVICE FOR THE INPUT DEVICE SUBFJ
)@@G@@MITTING THE @#@@@@.         RUN.    @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         THE OPTIFK
)@@G@@ONS SPECIFIED ARE APPLIED TO THE SYM STATEMENT USED   @G@@@@.         THFL
)@@G@@E 'U' OPTION (SAVE THE FILE) WILL BE PERMITTED ONLY IF THE  @G@@@@.     FM
)@@G@@    FILE USED ON BK1 WAS USER-DEFINED.  THE 'E' AND 'N' OPTIONS,  @G@@@@FN
)@@G@@.         WHICH ARE NOT USED BY @SYM, WILL CAUSE BK2 NOT TO SYM THE     FO
)@@G@@@G@@@@.         FILE.  THE 'E' OPTION WILL EXECUTE THE TEXT EDITOR ON THFP
)@@G@@E FILE@H@@@@.         SO THAT THE USER MAY EXAMINE THE FILE OF PRINT OUTFQ
)@@G@@PUT.  THE 'N'     @G@@@@.         OPTION WILL INHIBIT THE SYM AND LEAVE FR
)@@G@@THE FILE ASSIGNED TO    @F@@@@.         THE USER.  IF THE 'N' OR 'E' OPTFS
)@@G@@IONS ARE ON, BK2 WILL   @G@@@@.         ATTACH A USE NAME TO THE FILE FOFT

)@@G@@@G@@@@.         THE OPTIONS SPECIFIED ARE APPLIED TO THE SYM STATEMENT UHJ
)@@G@@SED   @G@@@@.         THE 'U' OPTION (SAVE THE FILE) WILL BE PERMITTED OHK
)@@G@@NLY IF THE  @G@@@@.         FILE USED ON BK1 WAS USER-DEFINED.  THE 'E' HL
)@@G@@AND 'N' OPTIONS,  @G@@@@.         WHICH ARE NOT USED BY @SYM, WILL CAUSEHM
)@@G@@ BK2 NOT TO SYM THE     @G@@@@.         FILE.  THE 'E' OPTION WILL EXECUHN
)@@G@@TE THE TEXT EDITOR ON THE FILE@H@@@@.         SO THAT THE USER MAY EXAMIHO
)@@G@@NE THE FILE OF PRINT OUTPUT.  THE 'N'     @G@@@@.         OPTION WILL INHP
)@@G@@HIBIT THE SYM AND LEAVE THE FILE ASSIGNED TO    @F@@@@.         THE USERHQ
)@@G@@.  IF THE 'N' OR 'E' OPTIONS ARE ON, BK2 WILL   @G@@@@.         ATTACH AHR
)@@G@@ USE NAME TO THE FILE FOR THE USER'S CONVENIENCE.     @F@@@@.         IFHS

)@@G@@IS USE NAME.  IF OMITTED, THE DEFAULT USE NAME WILL   @^@@@@.         BEHU

)@@G@@ED TO PERMIT EXAMINATION OR   @H@@@@.         MANIPULATION OF THE BREAKPHZ

)@@G@@1 FORMS THE FIRST PART OF THE PROCESSOR PAIR BK1 AND BK2.   @H@@@@.     YO
)@@G@@    BK1 PERMITS THE USER TO BREAKPOINT THE PRINT FILE WITHOUT DELVING   YP
)@@G@@@H@@@@.         INTO THE MYSTERIES OF OF CATALOGUED FILES, BREAKPOINT, AYQ
)@@G@@ND SYM.     @H@@@@.         BK1 IS CALLED TO ESTABLISH BREAKPOINT MODE; YR
)@@G@@ANY OUTPUT FOLLOWING    @G@@@@.         THE BK1 STATEMENT WILL BE DIVERTYS
)@@G@@ED.  THE FORM OF THE CONTROL  @^@@@@.         STATEMENT IS: @[@@@@.     YT
)@@G@@@D@@@@.              @BK1,OPTS FILE.,EQT/GRAN,REEL,RETENTION@[@@@@.     YU
)@@G@@@G@@@@.         FILE SPECIFIES THE FILE NAME TO WHICH THE OUTPUT IS TO BYV
)@@G@@E     @F@@@@.         SENT.  IF THE FILE IS ALREADY ASSIGNED TO THE RUN,YW
)@@G@@ THE  @G@@@@.         BREAKPOINT IS SIMPLY PERFORMED.  IF THE NAMED FILEYX
)@@G@@ IS NOT     @G@@@@.         ASSIGNED TO THE RUN, IT IS DYNAMICALLY ASSIGYY
)@@G@@NED, USING THE    @F@@@@.         OPTIONS, EQUIPMENT TYPE, MAX GRANULES,YZ
)@@G@@ REEL NUMBER, AND @G@@@@.         RETENTION SPECIFIED ON THE BK1 CARD.  ZA
)@@G@@OF COURSE, THE GRANULE  @G@@@@.         FIELD IS MEANINGFUL ONLY IF THE ZB
)@@G@@FILE IS MASS STORAGE, AND THE @H@@@@.         REEL AND RETENTION FIELDS ZC
)@@G@@ARE MEANINGFUL ONLY FOR TAPE.  THE ONLY   @G@@@@.         DEPARTURES FROZD
)@@G@@M SYSTEM STANDARDS ARE THAT THE FIELD AFTER THE @G@@@@.         EQUIPMENZE
)@@G@@T TYPE IS A MAX GRANULES RATHER THAN INITIAL RESERVE  @H@@@@.         FIZF
)@@G@@ELD, AND THAT IF ALL OPTIONS ARE OMITTED, THE OPTIONS C,P,R, AND G@ @@@@ZG
)@@G@@.         WILL BE ASSUMED.    @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.         IF ALL SPECIFIZH
)@@G@@CATIONS ARE OMITTED FROM THE BK1 STATEMENT,     @G@@@@.         A UNIQUEZI
)@@G@@ FILE NAME WILL BE CREATED, AND OUTPUT WILL BE SENT TO@F@@@@.         THZJ
)@@G@@AT FILE.  THUS IN THE CASE OF A DEMAND USER WISHING TO@F@@@@.         CRZK
)@@G@@EATE BATCH OUTPUT, THE STATEMENT USED IS SIMPLY: @BK1 @[@@@@.     @[@@@@ZL
)@@G@@.     @G@@@@.         IF TAG PRINFO$ SHOULD BE SET TO THE ER CODE OF THEZM
)@@G@@ WALKER     @G@@@@.         LOCAL CODE ER PRINFO$.  THIS ER PERMITS THE ZN
)@@G@@RUN TO RETRIEVE   @G@@@@.         PAGES USED SO FAR.  THIS IS USED TO PEZO
)@@G@@RMIT BK2 TO DISPLAY     @G@@@@.         THE NUMBER OF PAGES CREATED IN BZP
)@@G@@REAKPOINT MODE.  IF PRINFO$   @G@@@@.         IS SET TO ZERO, ALL LOCAL ZQ
)@@G@@CODE WILL BE REMOVED AND THE PAGE   @G@@@@.         COUNT FEATURE WILL NZR
)@@G@@OT BE AVAILABLE.  NOTE:  THE PAGE COUNT   @G@@@@.         IS AVAILABLE OZS
)@@G@@NLY WHEN BREAKPOINTING TO A CATALOGUED FILE.    @[@@@@.     %#@@@@-41   ZT
)@@G@@       BK1  @C@@[@.         MODIFICATION MADE JAN 76 BY N. GROSCH @E@@[@ZU
